CREATEEGG_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_602;When a card bearing this sigil is played, an Egg is created on the opposing space.;使用带有该印记的卡牌时，对面位置会出现一颗蛋。
DOUBLESTRIKE_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_275;A card bearing this sigil will strike the opposing space an extra time when attacking.;带有该印记的卡牌会在攻击时额外攻击对面位置一次。
GAINATTACKONKILL_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_163;When a card bearing this sigil attacks an opposing creature and it perishes, this card gains 1 power.;带有该印记的卡牌击杀对面的造物后，会获得1点力量。
HYDRAEGG_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_095;A card bearing this sigil hatches when drawn if the numbers 1 to 5 are represented in the health of creatures in your deck, and in their power, and if there is a creature of each tribe in your deck.;带有该印记的卡牌在抽取时的孵化条件如下：你的牌组中的造物的生命和力量包含1至5五个数字，且每个族群的造物都有一张。
MADEOFSTONE_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_046;A card bearing this sigil is immune to the effects of Touch of Death and Stinky.;带有该印记的卡牌可免疫死神之触和臭臭的印记效果。
MORSEL_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_754;When a card bearing this sigil is sacrificed, it adds its stat values to the card it was sacrificed for.;当带有该印记的卡牌被献祭时，它的状态值会被添加在献祭来的新卡上。
OPPONENTBONES_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_456;While a card bearing this sigil is on the board, opposing creatures also provide bones when perishing.;带有该印记的卡牌在牌桌上出现时，它对面的造物死亡时也会产生兽骨。
STRAFESWAP_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_364;At the end of the owner's turn, a card bearing this sigil will move in the direction inscribed in the sigil. Creatures in the way will be thrown back behind it.;持牌人回合结束时，带有该印记的卡牌会按照印记标记的方向突进。沿途的造物会被丢到它身后。
BONESSTATICON_GBCDESCRIPTION_C_426;The power of a card bearing this sigil is equal to half of the Bones of the owner.;带有该印记的卡牌的力量等于持牌人持有兽骨数量的一半。
